UPDATE:
You don't really know how good the food is until you try the same dish at different restaurants. I've had the shrimp burrito at different places, but Coyote's shrimp burrito has a LOT more flavor and makes me come back again and again. Son still enjoys their super nachos with steak and my husband still loves their chicken fajitas. Whenever we want Mexican food, this is where we go.
####################
My family loves the food here. I don't know why it took so long to try their food! My son loves their nachos with steak, I love the shrimp burrito, and my husband loves their chicken fajitas. We need to change things up but it's hard to pick something other than what you start craving for. Free chips and yummy salsa.< /Review>

<date>1329806935380</date><review>Love this store! They have a great selection of genres that interest me and their stock rotates more frequently than most used book stores. I have found more than a couple obscure titles that I had been keeping an eye out for there, and the harder-to-find books behind the counter resemble recommendations from the community. It is a very comfortable store, with good soft-playing music that follows you through the shelves. Children's art work and traditional orange-crate labels decorate the walls. The prices are very affordable, and the friendly service provided by the owners makes you feel right at home. If you haven't been here, then go. It is truly a store for the community. < Review>
My fiancÃ© and I come here at least once a year and stay for several hours just looking around and reading. It's a tiny hole in the wall, you have to know where you're going to find it because it's behind another shop, and it's a little old/dingy dirty. Apart from those things, WE LOVE IT. It's one of our favorite used bookstores in SoCal! They've got things sorted by topic and then by author name, they help you find stuff and are super sweet when you come in. Pricing is pretty cheap - the material is good quality, so it's not ridiculously low, but it's what you'd expect for used books. The whole shop has an owl theme too which is really fun and quirky. Love this place!<//Review>

I was referred to this OBGYN by my PCP. I scheduled my appointment when my authorization came in, which was mid-February. As with most doctors (especially in the high desert), they were booked out almost 2 months. No big deal...to be expected. So I made my appt for the first week in April, put it in my calendar on my phone, and set my reminder. Fast forward to the morning of my appt... I drive 45 minutes from my house to this appt, arrive 15 minutes prior to my appt time, and take a seat and wait to hear my name called. Only it's not.... and I'm watching person after person arrive and be called back. I wait until I've sat for half an hour, approach the woman at the front desk, and ask her if she needs to see my insurance card and have me fill out paperwork. She asks my name, to which I tell her, and she proceeds to tell me that "they were just about to call me up" (mmmhmmm) and do I recall getting a voicemail they left on such and such date at such and such time. When I tell her I hadn't heard any voicemail, she proceeds to let me know that because I never returned the call to confirm the appt, they cancelled it. COME AGAIN?? I ask her why they would take it upon themselves to cancel an appointment without my having actually been reached to advise of such cancellation,  and she explains that it's just their policy due to having so many no show appointments and a high wait list of people wanting last minute appointments. Now don't get me wrong, I can appreciate a doctor's office that accommodates patients who can't wait 2-3 months to be seen.....WHEN A PATIENT WHO SCHEDULES THE APPOINTMENT CANCELS SAID APPOINTMENT!!!!  I never cancelled, and have never been expected to confirm an appointment in order for it to be considered an actual real appointment. How do they know they called the right number? How do they know I had access to my phone or my voicemail? I could have been traveling (which isn't a stretch, I frequently do go on a cruise or an airplane). The point being, I was at the appointment that I took the time to make two months ago. It's not my problem if other people don't know how to anticipate a wait and book a doctor appointment in advance, and furthermore, I shouldn't have to do another step in this process to "confirm back" in order for that appointment I made to count. This is another case, in my opinion, where those of us who are responsible and organized get punished with unrealistic and unreasonable "policies" that come about as a result of folks who aren't. Horrible customer service. Oh wait, I didn't even touch on WHY THEY LET ME SIT FROM 10:18-10:45 before so kindly letting me know THEY CANCELLED MY APPOINTMENT FOR NO DANG GOOD REASON. Good thing I went up to the desk, I could have sat there all day. No thanks, this so called office couldn't pay me to be a patient there.<//text>

<gmapID>0x80c49f5f2684da9d:0xf19e9f11f34ae7bb<//gmapID><Review>I switched to this OBGYN office after leaving a nearby facility.  I must say, the difference is well... refreshing.  The doctor is knowledgeable, decisive, and all encompassing.  I really like dealing with him, and although he's got a million patients in the waiting room, he answers every question you may have.

The office staff is second to none.  They are all personable, treat you wonderfully and explain everything.  The common theme with them and the doctor is that everyone is incredibly thorough.  Although the fees are just as high as the other office I left, the billing department comes and provides you with a full fee schedule tailored to your needs.  You know what you'll be expected to pay and when.  They answer all phone calls (quickly I might add), and they route any concerns you have to the doctor.  I've always received a personable call back either from the doctor, or them relaying the doctor's information.  There are PAs here at the office, so I do believe you see them from time to time.  Although I've had 3 OB appointments now, and I've only seen the doctor.  I'm super partial to him, so I hope I get to keep seeing him over my pregnancy.

They have top notch equipment in the office, including a very advanced ultrasound machine.  They even do NT ultrasounds for the mothers who are going through 1st and 2nd trimester screening.  If you've had a baby before, you know that a doctor's office who does NT ultrasounds is EXTREMELY rare.  Everyone I know, including myself, has had to go to a specialist to have this performed.  Ultrasounds are done here on Saturday, and the ultrasound room has ample space to bring a family member or two.  They also do 4D ultrasounds in the event you want to pay extra.  On a regular OB visit, if they ever can't find the baby's heartbeat, they nab you and pull you immediately into the U/S room and perform a quick U/S.  You never have to wonder if the baby is OK upon leaving their office.

I do have one gripe.  Only one so far, kinda amazing.  Doctor's offices now do infant circumcision, as they are no longer done at the hospital.  Office walls are very thin, and when a pregnant mom comes in for a prenatal appointment, we are all excited for what's next.  To hear a blood curdling scream down the hall from an infant baby, we all know what's going on.  COMPLETELY breaks our mommy/daddy hearts and changes the mood of our doctor appointments.

Other than that, this office is a diamond in the rough in the desert.  I couldn't be happier to have been referred there by friends.</Review><userid>114783422064134462275<//userid><Date>1482381439440< /Date>< Rating>

< text>
Have been going to this church for several years now.  Had a bit of healing to do, and this church allowed that process for me and my family.   I love the real Biblical teaching, without the fluff added in, and the pastors are excellent in presenting the Word in a clear and concise manner.
My children are both grown, so I don't have much to say about that area - other than it appears to be run very well, and with a slew of volunteers.  Lots of young families in the church, so they must be doing something right.
The church focuses on small groups as well, which is a good thing if you have the time to be in one, but so far we have not found a match for our lifestyle.  Sunday school offerings are good - my parents really enjoy their group.  Parking can be a challenge - but only if you go to the 9ish service.  I try to go to the earlier service and do not find parking to be an issue then.<//text>

<userid>105046375998782625877<//userid>< text>
Great church for those looking to get plugged in to a small group and make some friends in Christ. "Life Groups," as LBF calls them, are one of the best parts of this church. You get great teaching on Sundays and an in-depth analysis during the week when you meet with your group. I'm much more engaged in the sermons because I know in a couple days I'll get to talk about it with a group of people I have a lot in common with, and whom I can now truly call my friends.

Life Bible Fellowship is a wonderful, spirit-filled group of believers who don't flinch at the hard issues of life and the Bible, follow Jesus in everything they do, and show love to all. I've been a part of this church for three years now, and I'm so glad I gave it a chance when we started looking in the area.</text>

< Review>
I took a 2-hour driving lesson last Friday with the instructor "Zain" and he was so awesome.

Basically, I got my driving license in NY and I barely had driving experience other than road training sessions. Driving here is so much different from NY, so I thought it would be great to have 2-3 sessions.

Price-wise, this driving school is so reasonable and transparent because I saw so many driving schools with too expensive rates or no rate information.

With my instructor Zain, I learned so many driving tips within 2 hours. I felt like he knows how to teach people and point out important things concisely and precisely. Also, he's quite a good talker, so it was very pleasant.

I will take another lesson with him.

One downside of driving school is that it is hard to talk to the representative. Once I got connected, he was so very nice, but many times my call just transferred to the voice mail. Maybe they are too busy.

Overall, I highly recommend this place and my instructor Zain.</Review>

<Resp>None</Resp>< Review>
I write for a music and coffee blog called Crooners In Coffeeshops, in which I interview local musicians at local coffeeshops. My writeup reflects the positive experience that I encountered at Caffe Luxxe on our interview date.

L.A. based small batch coffee roaster Caffe Luxxe is wonderful example of what can grow from the powerful bond of friendship, specifically one that spans decades like that of owners Mark Wain and Gary Chau. Taking the chance to quit their corporate jobs in 2006, theyâ€™ve been able to fuel their business from their personal relationship and their love for European luxury caffe culture.

A fun fact, Caffe Luxxe is the first of its kind in L.A. for artisan coffee preparation, and boy golly, it is not one to miss at any of its So Cal locations. The coffee world is your oyster when picking your beverage of choice from their delectable menu of drips, pour overs, and a unique variety of Bevande Di Caffe (including a chocolate-y shaken Caffe Shakerato, a sparkling espresso Caffe Frizzante, and a spiced citrus Caffe Nico). If seasonal specials are your thing, have no fear, because theyâ€™ve got those covered too! What more could you ask for?< /Review>
